	function FPSBooster()
		local v411 = true;
		local v412 = game;
		local v413 = v412.Workspace;
		local v414 = v412.Lighting;
		local v415 = v413.Terrain;
		sethiddenproperty(v414, "Technology", 2);
		sethiddenproperty(v415, "Decoration", false);
		v415.WaterWaveSize = 0 + 0;
		v415.WaterWaveSpeed = 0;
		v415.WaterReflectance = 0;
		v415.WaterTransparency = 1355 - (117 + 1238);
		v414.GlobalShadows = false;
		v414.FogEnd = 9000001203 - (686 + 1029);
		v414.Brightness = 0;
		settings().Rendering.QualityLevel = "Level01";
		for v552, v553 in pairs(v412:GetDescendants()) do
			if (v553:IsA("Part") or v553:IsA("Union") or v553:IsA("CornerWedgePart") or v553:IsA("TrussPart")) then
				local v697 = 1356 - (1074 + 282);
				local v698;
				while true do
					if (v697 == (1617 - (1359 + 258))) then
						v698 = 0 - 0;
						while true do
							if (v698 == 0) then
								v553.Material = "Plastic";
								v553.Reflectance = 1935 - (1730 + 205);
								break;
							end
						end
						break;
					end
				end
			elseif (v553:IsA("Decal") or (v553:IsA("Texture") and v411)) then
				v553.Transparency = 529 - (67 + 461);
			elseif (v553:IsA("ParticleEmitter") or v553:IsA("Trail")) then
				v553.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(0 - 0);
			elseif v553:IsA("Explosion") then
				local v1160 = 0 - 0;
				local v1161;
				while true do
					if ((0 - 0) == v1160) then
						v1161 = 0;

function getAllBladeHitsPlayers(v178)
	local v179 = 1120 - (242 + 878);
	local v180;
	local v181;
	local v182;
	while true do
		local v441 = 1783 - (1395 + 388);
		while true do
			if (0 == v441) then
				if (v179 == 2) then
					return v180;
				end
				if (v179 == 0) then
					v180 = {};
					v181 = game.Players.LocalPlayer;
					v179 = 1 + 0;
				end
				v441 = 1 + 0;
			end
			if (v441 == 1) then
				if (v179 == (1 + 0)) then
					local v828 = 0 + 0;
					while true do
						if (v828 == (1948 - (1289 + 658))) then
							v179 = 2 + 0;
							break;
						end
						if ((0 - 0) == v828) then
							v182 = game:GetService("Workspace").Characters:GetChildren();
							for v1183 = 1 + 0, #v182 do
								local v1184 = 0;
								local v1185;
								local v1186;
								local v1187;
								while true do
									if (v1184 == (0 + 0)) then
										v1185 = 0 - 0;
										v1186 = nil;
										v1184 = 1977 - (337 + 1639);
									end
									if (v1184 == (1 + 0)) then
										v1187 = nil;
										while true do
											if (v1185 == (0 - 0)) then
												v1186 = v182[v1183];
												v1187 = v1186:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid");
												v1185 = 2 - 1;
											end
											if (v1185 == 1) then
												if ((v1186.Name ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name) and v1187 and v1187.RootPart and (v1187.Health > (0 - 0)) and (v181:DistanceFromCharacter(v1187.RootPart.Position) < (v178 + (1742 - (630 + 1107))))) then
													table.insert(v180, v1187.RootPart);
												end
												break;
											end
										end
										break;
									end
								end
							end
							v828 = 1;
						end
					end
				end
				break;
			end
		end
	end
end
function getAllBladeHits(v183)
	local v184 = {};
	local v185 = game.Players.LocalPlayer;
	local v186 = game:GetService("Workspace").Enemies:GetChildren();
	for v442 = 1, #v186 do
		local v443 = v186[v442];
		local v444 = v443:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid");
		if (v444 and v444.RootPart and (v444.Health > (0 + 0)) and (v185:DistanceFromCharacter(v444.RootPart.Position) < (v183 + 5))) then
			table.insert(v184, v444.RootPart);
		end
	end
	return v184;
